<script>
  (function() {
    const slider = document.getElementById('dydd-slider');
    const track = document.querySelector('.dydd-slider-track');
    const slides = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dydd-testimonial-card'));
    const prevBtn = document.querySelector('.dydd-prev');
    const nextBtn = document.querySelector('.dydd-next');
    const dots = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dydd-dot'));

    if (!slider || !track || !slides.length) return;

    let index = 0;
    let intervalId = null;
    const delay = 7000;

    function updateSlider() {
      track.style.transform = 'translateX(-' + (index * 100) + '%)';
      dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
        dot.classList.toggle('is-active', i === index);
      });
    }

    function goToSlide(i) {
      index = (i + slides.length) % slides.length;
      updateSlider();
    }

    function startAutoRotate() {
      stopAutoRotate();
      intervalId = setInterval(() => {
        goToSlide(index + 1);
      }, delay);
    }

    function stopAutoRotate() {
      if (intervalId) {
        clearInterval(intervalId);
        intervalId = null;
      }
    }

    if (prevBtn) prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      goToSlide(index - 1);
      startAutoRotate();
    });

    if (nextBtn) nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      goToSlide(index + 1);
      startAutoRotate();
    });

    dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
      dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
        goToSlide(i);
        startAutoRotate();
      });
    });

    slider.addEventListener('mouseenter', stopAutoRotate);
    slider.addEventListener('mouseleave', startAutoRotate);
    slider.addEventListener('focusin', stopAutoRotate);
    slider.addEventListener('focusout', startAutoRotate);

    updateSlider();
    startAutoRotate();
  })();
</script>

  // ---------- DOM ----------
  var searchEl  = document.getElementById("sg-search");
  var selectEl  = document.getElementById("sg-select");
  var leftList  = document.getElementById("sg-left-list");
  var rightList = document.getElementById("sg-right-list");
  var wrap      = document.getElementById("sg-wrap");

  function clearLists(){
    leftList.innerHTML = "";
    rightList.innerHTML = "";
  }

  // Render both columns for given names (array of gift names). If empty/null => all.
  function renderGifts(names){
    clearLists();

    var set = [];
    var i,g;

    if(!names || !names.length){
      set = GIFTS.slice(0);
    } else {
      for(i=0;i<GIFTS.length;i++){
        g = GIFTS[i];
        if(names.indexOf(g.name) !== -1){
          set.push(g);
        }
      }
    }

    for(i=0;i<set.length;i++){
      g = set[i];

      // LEFT (definition + scripture)
      var lb = document.createElement("button");
      lb.className = "acc-btn";
      lb.setAttribute("data-gift", g.name);
      lb.setAttribute("aria-expanded","false");
      lb.innerHTML = g.name + ' <span class="acc-caret">▶</span>';

      var lp = document.createElement("div");
      lp.className = "acc-panel";
      lp.setAttribute("data-gift", g.name);
      lp.innerHTML =
        '<p><strong>Definition:</strong> ' + g.definition + '</p>' +
        '<p><strong>Scripture:</strong> ' + g.scriptures + '</p>';

      leftList.appendChild(lb);
      leftList.appendChild(lp);

      // RIGHT (four reflection correlation statements)
      var rb = document.createElement("button");
      rb.className = "acc-btn";
      rb.setAttribute("data-gift", g.name);
      rb.setAttribute("aria-expanded","false");
      rb.innerHTML = g.name + ' <span class="acc-caret">▶</span>';

      var rp = document.createElement("div");
      rp.className = "acc-panel";
      rp.setAttribute("data-gift", g.name);

      function reflectionRow(refName){
        var text = (g.reflections && g.reflections[refName]) ? g.reflections[refName] : "—";
        return (
          '<div class="ref-row">' +
            '<span class="pill pill-' + refName + '">' + refName + '</span>' +
            '<span class="ref-label">' + text + '</span>' +
          '</div>'
        );
      }

      rp.innerHTML =
        '<div class="ref-rows">' +
          reflectionRow("Architect") +
          reflectionRow("Artisan") +
          reflectionRow("Shepherd") +
          reflectionRow("Steward") +
        '</div>';

      rightList.appendChild(rb);
      rightList.appendChild(rp);
    }
  }

// Accordion behavior + GLOBAL sync (only one gift open at a time)
wrap.onclick = function(e){
  var target = e.target;

  while(target && !target.classList.contains("acc-btn")){
    target = target.parentNode;
  }
  if(!target){ return; }

  var giftName = target.getAttribute("data-gift");
  var isOpen = target.classList.contains("active");

  // Get all matching buttons (left + right)
  var allMatching = wrap.querySelectorAll('.acc-btn[data-gift="'+giftName+'"]');

  if(isOpen){
    // CLOSE both sides for this gift
    for(var i=0;i<allMatching.length;i++){
      var btn = allMatching[i];
      btn.classList.remove("active");
      btn.setAttribute("aria-expanded","false");
      var panel = btn.nextElementSibling;
      if(panel){ panel.style.display = "none"; }
    }
    return;
  }

  // OPEN case:
  // 1) Close EVERYTHING currently open (both columns)
  var allBtns = wrap.querySelectorAll(".acc-btn");
  for(var j=0;j<allBtns.length;j++){
    allBtns[j].classList.remove("active");
    allBtns[j].setAttribute("aria-expanded","false");
    var p = allBtns[j].nextElementSibling;
    if(p && p.classList.contains("acc-panel")){
      p.style.display = "none";
    }
  }

  // 2) Open the matching pair (left + right)
  for(var k=0;k<allMatching.length;k++){
    var btn2 = allMatching[k];
    btn2.classList.add("active");
    btn2.setAttribute("aria-expanded","true");
    var panel2 = btn2.nextElementSibling;
    if(panel2){ panel2.style.display = "block"; }
  }
};



  // Search box: filter which <option> items are visible and update columns
  function getVisibleOptionNames(){
    var opts = selectEl.options;
    var names = [];
    for(var i=0;i<opts.length;i++){
      if(opts[i].style.display !== "none"){
        names.push(opts[i].value);
      }
    }
    return names;
  }

  searchEl.oninput = function(){
    var q = searchEl.value.toLowerCase();
    var opts = selectEl.options;

    for(var i=0;i<opts.length;i++){
      var txt = opts[i].text.toLowerCase();
      if(!q || txt.indexOf(q) !== -1){
        opts[i].style.display = "";
      } else {
        opts[i].style.display = "none";
        opts[i].selected = false;
      }
    }

    var visibleNames = getVisibleOptionNames();
    renderGifts(visibleNames.length ? visibleNames : null);
  };

  // Multi-select change: show selected gifts, or visible if none selected
  selectEl.onchange = function(){
    var opts = selectEl.options;
    var selectedNames = [];
    for(var i=0;i<opts.length;i++){
      if(opts[i].selected && opts[i].style.display !== "none"){
        selectedNames.push(opts[i].value);
      }
    }
    if(selectedNames.length){
      renderGifts(selectedNames);
    } else {
      var visibleNames = getVisibleOptionNames();
      renderGifts(visibleNames.length ? visibleNames : null);
    }
  };

  // Initial render: show all gifts
  renderGifts(null);
})();
</script>

            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Text -->
          <div class="dyabout-textCol">
            <div class="dyabout-kicker">Who We Are</div>
            <h2 class="dyabout-title">A Journey Rooted in Purpose</h2>

            <p class="dyabout-p">
              Discover Your Divine Design was created by John Willoughby, a leader, coach, and devoted follower of Christ
              who believes every person has been created by God with purpose, on purpose.
              Through years of serving leaders, churches, and teams, John recognized a common need:
              many believers longed for greater clarity about who they are and how to faithfully live out their calling.
            </p>

            <p class="dyabout-p">
              That desire gave rise to Discover Your Divine Design. Drawing from experience in leadership development,
              biblical teaching, and personal growth, John built a process that is rooted in Scripture and shaped for real life.
              More than a book or program, DYDD is a guided journey that helps people explore their identity, expertise, story,
              desires, spiritual gifts, and niche within the Body of Christ.
            </p>

            <p class="dyabout-p">
              At its heart, Discover Your Divine Design exists to help people grow in clarity, confidence, and courage
              as they live out the life God has entrusted to them — in the church, at home, and in the world.
            </p>
          </div>

        </div>

    <!-- =========================
         3. FAQ
    ========================== -->
    <section class="dyfaq">
      <header class="dyfaq-head">
        <h2 class="dyfaq-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
        <p class="dyfaq-sub">
          A few helpful answers about what we believe, how DYDD works, and the heart behind this journey.
        </p>
      </header>

      <div class="dyfaq-list">

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">What is our statement of faith?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            We believe the Bible is the inspired and authoritative Word of God and the ultimate guide for faith and life (2 Timothy 3:16–17). We believe in one God, eternally existing in three persons: Father, Son, and Holy Spirit (Matthew 28:19).
            <br><br>
            We believe salvation is a gift of God’s grace, received through faith in Jesus Christ alone—who lived a sinless life, died for our sins, and rose again to offer eternal life to all who believe (John 3:16; Ephesians 2:8–9).
            <br><br>
            We believe the Holy Spirit indwells every believer, equipping and empowering them to live a godly life and serve in the advancement of God’s Kingdom (Acts 1:8; 1 Corinthians 12:4–7).
            <br><br>
            We believe the Church is the Body of Christ, called to unity, love, and service, and that every believer is gifted by God to build up the Body and glorify Him (Romans 12:4–6; Ephesians 4:11–13).
            <br><br>
            We believe Jesus Christ will return to fulfill all of God’s promises, bringing final restoration and eternal life with Him to all who belong to Him (Revelation 21:1–5).
          </div>
        </details>

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">What do we believe about the Bible?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            We believe the Bible is the inspired and authoritative Word of God, fully trustworthy and the final authority in all matters of faith and life (2 Timothy 3:16–17). It is the foundation for everything we teach and the standard that guides our process.
          </div>
        </details>

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">What makes our approach unique?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            We integrate biblical truth with practical tools that help people see how their identity, expertise, story, desires, and spiritual gifts fit together.
            <br><br>
            DesignID serves as a reflective lens that helps reveal both natural strengths and areas for growth. When these elements are understood together, people gain clarity about how they can faithfully contribute within the Body of Christ.
          </div>
        </details>

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">How do you help people discover their design?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            Through guided reflection, assessments, and biblical teaching, we walk people through six key areas: Identity, Expertise, Story, Desire, Spiritual Gifts, and Niche.
            <br><br>
            Each area reveals part of how God has been shaping your life. When they come together, people begin to see more clearly where they can serve and contribute within the Body of Christ.
          </div>
        </details>

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">What if I’m not sure where I fit in the Church?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            That uncertainty is more common than people realize, and it is exactly why this journey exists.
            <br><br>
            Discover Your Divine Design helps people see how God has uniquely shaped them so they can step into meaningful participation within the Body of Christ with confidence and clarity.
          </div>
        </details>

        <details class="dyfaq-item">
          <summary class="dyfaq-question">Is Discover Your Divine Design affiliated with a specific denomination?</summary>
          <div class="dyfaq-answer">
            Discover Your Divine Design is rooted in historic Christian faith and grounded in Scripture. While it is not tied to one specific denomination, it is designed to serve believers, churches, and ministries that affirm the authority of the Bible and the centrality of Jesus Christ.
          </div>
        </details>

      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- =========================

<script>
(function () {
  const pages = [
    {
      title: "DesignID Cover Page",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823072027-D39WPA5O4U27SSTN6QS9/DesignID+Report+Cover+Page.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "DesignID Overview",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823072107-E0M2HIN612WCMKJ5KST2/DesignID+Report+Page+2.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Personal Profile",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823072944-V2RAGYDRC35UIBOYV4X3/DesignID+Report+Page+3.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Primary & Secondary Reflections",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823073249-YJTYSW50SRKRJNP0I0K3/DesignID+Report+Page+4.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Integrative Reflections Introduction",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823073989-M1I9DD6NA2L87MI7RMS0/DesignID+Report+Page+5.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Integrative Reflection Details",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823074272-6B5TADG3AH6PVTB2JMRE/DesignID+Report+Page+6.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Reflection Bandwidth Introduction",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823074975-MK3VBHMOEMRRDRMNBP17/DesignID+Report+Page+7.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Reflection Bandwidth Guide",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823075425-20QXTAMWOEGYHOMBYO56/DesignID+Report+Page+8.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Learning & Contribution",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823076379-3ZC2GDL8KJ8O9EA9BJA9/DesignID+Report+Page+9.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Shadow Reflection",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823077316-PMKPUXEX49LUCX6WVMH6/DesignID+Report+Page+10.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Reflection Summary",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823077570-O6DNB9NRYAKRY8DQ45PG/DesignID+Report+Page+11.jpg?format=500w"
    },
    {
      title: "Integrating with Discover Your Divine Design",
      src: "https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/1772823078343-ZFFLJN81DCRA2GJSZVU1/DesignID+Report+Page+12.jpg?format=500w"
    }
  ];

  const mainImage = document.getElementById('dyidMainImage');
  const pageCount = document.getElementById('dyidPageCount');
  const prevBtn = document.getElementById('dyidPrevBtn');
  const nextBtn = document.getElementById('dyidNextBtn');

  if (!mainImage || !pageCount || !prevBtn || !nextBtn) return;

  let currentIndex = 0;

  function updateSlider() {
    const current = pages[currentIndex];
    mainImage.style.opacity = '0.25';

    const preload = new Image();
    preload.onload = function () {
      mainImage.src = current.src;
      mainImage.alt = current.title;
      mainImage.style.opacity = '1';
    };
    preload.src = current.src;

    pageCount.textContent = 'Page ' + (currentIndex + 1) + ' of ' + pages.length;
    prevBtn.disabled = currentIndex === 0;
    nextBtn.disabled = currentIndex === pages.length - 1;
  }

  prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (currentIndex > 0) {
      currentIndex--;
      updateSlider();
    }
  });

  nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (currentIndex < pages.length - 1) {
      currentIndex++;
      updateSlider();
    }
  });

  updateSlider();
})();
</script>

  <h1 class="dypd-title">Move from understanding your design to applying it with clarity</h1>

  <p class="dypd-sub">
    DesignPD helps you understand how you naturally <strong>Plan, Decide, and Do</strong>. Built on the foundation of
    DesignID, it brings your design into everyday life so you can see how your tendencies influence leadership,
    teamwork, decision making, and sustainable contribution.
  </p>

    <!-- WHAT DESIGNPD IS -->
    <section class="dypd-section">
      <div class="dypd-split dypd-splitTight">
        <div class="dypd-text">
          <div class="dypd-kicker">What Is DesignPD?</div>
          <h2 class="dypd-h2">A practical next step after DesignID</h2>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            DesignID helps you understand the way God’s design is reflected through you. It gives language to identity,
            reflection, and contribution. DesignPD takes the next step by helping you understand how that design tends
            to move in everyday life.
          </p>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            The <strong>PD</strong> in DesignPD can be understood as both <strong>Personal Development</strong> and
            <strong>Professional Development</strong>. The same tendencies that shape how you approach planning,
            decisions, and action at work also shape how you lead, relate, serve, and carry responsibility in the rest of life.
          </p>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            In that sense, DesignPD is where design becomes practical. It helps you see how your inner wiring becomes
            visible in your real patterns, especially when expectations rise, pressure builds, or collaboration becomes complex.
          </p>
        </div>

        <div class="dypd-sideArt">
          <div class="dypd-iconPanel">
            <div class="dypd-icon"
                 style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/b7a300e4-fe78-407a-abb5-290e0ff5c149/designpd-icon.png?format=2500w');">
            </div>
            <div class="dypd-iconCopy">
              <h3>Plan. Decide. Do.</h3>
              <p>
                Three simple movements that reveal how people naturally approach vision, choices, and execution.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

<!-- WHY DESIGNID FIRST -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <div class="dypd-highlight">
    <header class="dypd-head">
      <div class="dypd-kicker">Why DesignID Comes First</div>
      <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">DesignPD is strongest when it grows out of DesignID</h2>
      <p class="dypd-headSub">
        DesignPD is not a replacement for DesignID. It is a companion report that helps you apply what DesignID reveals.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dypd-grid2">
      <article class="dypd-miniCard dypd-miniCard-icon">
        <div class="dypd-miniIcon">
          <img src="https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/ca9324a6-b779-495d-bc73-a6cc667175e1/ID-icon-color+400.jpg?format=2500w" alt="DesignID icon">
        </div>

        <h3 class="dypd-h3">DesignID gives you the foundation</h3>
        <p class="dypd-p">
          DesignID helps you understand your reflections, integrative strengths, and bandwidth patterns. It answers
          the question, <strong>How has God designed me?</strong>
        </p>
      </article>

      <article class="dypd-miniCard dypd-miniCard-icon">
        <div class="dypd-miniIcon">
          <img src="https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/b7a300e4-fe78-407a-abb5-290e0ff5c149/designpd-icon.png?format=2500w" alt="DesignPD icon">
        </div>

        <h3 class="dypd-h3">DesignPD shows how that design moves</h3>
        <p class="dypd-p">
          DesignPD shows how your design tends to show up in action. It answers the question,
          <strong>How do I naturally plan, decide, and act?</strong>
        </p>
      </article>
    </div>

    <p class="dypd-p dypd-centerText">
      Together, they create a far more complete picture. DesignID gives you the language of design. DesignPD shows how that
      design is likely to function in leadership, teamwork, conflict, collaboration, and day to day responsibility.
    </p>
  </div>
</section>

    <!-- STORY ARC -->
    <section class="dypd-section">
      <header class="dypd-head">
        <div class="dypd-kicker">From Insight to Action</div>
        <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Why progression from DesignID to DesignPD is so powerful</h2>
        <p class="dypd-headSub">
          Many people can recognize parts of their design once they see their DesignID results. The next challenge is learning
          how that design actually operates in real life.
        </p>
      </header>

      <div class="dypd-storyGrid">
        <article class="dypd-storyCard">
          <div class="dypd-step">1</div>
          <h3>See your design</h3>

            DesignID helps you understand the reflections, blends, and strengths that shape how grace is expressed through your life.
          </p>
        </article>

        <article class="dypd-storyCard">
          <div class="dypd-step">2</div>
          <h3>Name your tendencies</h3>
          <p>
            DesignPD helps you recognize how those strengths tend to move when you are planning, making decisions, and getting things done.
          </p>
        </article>

        <article class="dypd-storyCard">
          <div class="dypd-step">3</div>

          <div class="dypd-step">4</div>
          <h3>Live In Alignment</h3>

          </p>
        </article>
      </div>
    </section>

<!-- THE THREE AXES -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <header class="dypd-head">
    <div class="dypd-kicker">The Three Core Movements</div>
    <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Plan, Decide, and Do</h2>
    <p class="dypd-headSub">
      DesignPD centers around three simple but powerful movements. Every person engages in all three, but each person tends
      to approach them a little differently. These patterns shape how you prepare, process, and move.
    </p>
  </header>

  <div class="dypd-axisStack">

    <!-- PLAN -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-plan">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-plan">PLAN</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you approach vision and execution</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-plan">
          <span>Dreamer</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Doer</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Plan axis looks at how you naturally approach preparation, momentum, and forward movement. Some people begin
          with imagination, possibilities, and future vision. Others begin with action, structure, and practical next steps.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Neither side is better. Dreamers help open possibilities. Doers help bring movement and traction. DesignPD helps
          you understand where you tend to begin and how that tendency affects the way you lead, prepare, and contribute.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-plan">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your planning tendency affects how you handle goals, priorities, meetings, change,
          and the pace at which ideas become action.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/3fb2e85d-d272-4f9f-9d0d-d7a21a1c5a2d/diverse-group-of-young-business-people-working-in-2026-03-18-05-03-41-utc+800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

    <!-- DECIDE -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-decide">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-decide">DECIDE</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you process choices and make decisions</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-decide">
          <span>Feel It</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Think It</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Decide axis looks at how you tend to process information when choices need to be made. Some people lead with
          instinct, empathy, and internal awareness. Others lead with analysis, objectivity, and careful evaluation.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Healthy decisions need both discernment and clarity. DesignPD helps reveal where you naturally start, which often
          explains why certain decisions feel obvious to you while others require more effort, more input, or more time.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-decide">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your decision tendency affects how you weigh options, handle tension, respond to people,
          and navigate moments where conviction and complexity meet.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/fc5e805d-692c-4e1a-ad30-d0280f5f760d/stressed-business-colleagues-having-a-meeting-in-a-2026-03-24-23-47-32-utc800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

    <!-- DO -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-do">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-do">DO</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you move work forward</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-do">
          <span>Solo</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Together</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Do axis looks at how you tend to carry responsibility and complete what is in front of you. Some people gain
          momentum through independent ownership. Others gain momentum through shared effort and collaboration.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Both styles bring value. Solo tendencies often create speed and ownership. Together tendencies often create shared
          clarity, stronger buy in, and broader engagement. DesignPD helps make those patterns visible so they can become strengths
          instead of friction points.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-do">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your doing tendency affects communication, delegation, follow through, accountability,
          and the way you contribute inside teams and relationships.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/96377b09-83ad-43d3-b83a-2cc50a6754ba/surfing-the-web-for-something-to-add-to-his-busine-2026-01-09-11-04-42-utc800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

  </div>
</section>

 <!-- PRACTICAL APPLICATIONS -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <header class="dypd-head">
    <div class="dypd-kicker">Practical Application</div>
    <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Where DesignPD becomes especially useful</h2>
    <p class="dypd-headSub">
      The report is designed to help you see how your Plan, Decide, and Do tendencies influence real life situations. These
      are the environments where your patterns often become most visible and most valuable to understand.
    </p>
  </header>

  <div class="dypd-appGrid">

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appConflict">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Conflict</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design tends to respond when tension rises</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        Understand how your tendencies shape the way you frame conflict, interpret what is happening, and respond when communication becomes strained.
      </p>
    </article>

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appCollab">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Collaboration</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design tends to work with others</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        See how you naturally contribute in group settings and where shared effort may feel energizing, difficult, or misunderstood.
      </p>
    </article>

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appLeadership">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Leadership</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design tends to influence direction and people</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        Gain clarity on how your leadership style is shaped by the way you plan, discern, and move priorities or people forward.
      </p>
    </article>

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appPressure">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Pressure</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design tends to respond under strain</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        Recognize what happens when your natural tendencies are stressed and how to respond with greater steadiness and awareness.
      </p>
    </article>

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appSustain">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Sustainability</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design tends to maintain strength over time</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        Learn how to work in ways that fit your God given tendencies rather than fighting them in ways that create unnecessary fatigue.
      </p>
    </article>

    <article class="dypd-appCard dypd-appAlign">
      <div class="dypd-appTop">
        <h3 class="dypd-appTitle">Alignment</h3>
        <p class="dypd-appSub">How your design and environment work together</p>
      </div>
      <p class="dypd-cardText">
        Understand how your design and tendencies work together so your contribution becomes more intentional, healthy, and effective.
      </p>
    </article>

  </div>
</section>

    <!-- INDIVIDUALS AND TEAMS -->
    <section class="dypd-section">
      <div class="dypd-grid2">
        <article class="dypd-bigCard">
          <div class="dypd-kicker">For Individuals</div>
          <h2 class="dypd-h2">See how you naturally operate</h2>
          <p class="dypd-p">
            DesignPD helps individuals understand why certain ways of working feel natural, why certain responsibilities feel heavier,
            and why certain team dynamics feel easy or difficult. It gives language to your tendencies so you can lead yourself better,
            communicate with greater clarity, and grow more intentionally.
          </p>
          <ul class="dypd-list">
            <li>Improve self awareness</li>
            <li>Strengthen leadership and communication</li>
            <li>Understand work style and decision patterns</li>
            <li>Recognize growth areas under pressure</li>
            <li>Build more sustainable contribution</li>
          </ul>
        </article>

        <article class="dypd-bigCard">
          <div class="dypd-kicker">For Teams</div>
          <h2 class="dypd-h2">Understand how people work differently</h2>
          <p class="dypd-p">
            DesignPD helps teams move beyond vague personality observations into practical understanding. It reveals how different
            people approach planning, decisions, and execution so teams can communicate better, reduce friction, and value one another’s
            contribution more clearly.
          </p>
          <ul class="dypd-list">
            <li>Improve collaboration and role clarity</li>
            <li>Reduce unnecessary misunderstanding</li>
            <li>Strengthen meetings and decision flow</li>
            <li>Support healthier leadership conversations</li>
            <li>Create more balanced team contribution</li>
          </ul>
        </article>

<!-- FAQ SECTION -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <div class="dypd-faqWrap">
    <header class="dypd-head">
      <div class="dypd-kicker">Frequently Asked Questions</div>
      <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Questions about DesignPD</h2>
      <p class="dypd-headSub">
        A few helpful answers before you begin your DesignPD report.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dypd-faqList">

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Do I need to complete DesignID before DesignPD?</summary>
        <p>
          Yes. DesignPD is designed to build on the foundation of DesignID. DesignID helps you understand your design,
          while DesignPD helps you understand how that design tends to show up in planning, decision making, and action.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>What does DesignPD measure?</summary>
        <p>
          DesignPD explores how you naturally Plan, Decide, and Do. It looks at tendencies such as vision and execution,
          intuition and analysis, and independent or collaborative action.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Is DesignPD for personal development or professional development?</summary>
        <p>
          It can support both. DesignPD helps individuals grow in self-awareness while also helping leaders and teams
          understand how people work, communicate, decide, and contribute together.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>How can teams use DesignPD?</summary>
        <p>
          Teams can use DesignPD to better understand differences in planning, decision making, collaboration, leadership,
          pressure, and sustainability. This can reduce misunderstanding and support healthier alignment.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Is DesignPD a personality test?</summary>
        <p>
          No. DesignPD is not meant to label or limit you. It is a reflection tool that helps you recognize patterns in
          how your design tends to move into everyday action.
        </p>
      </details>

    </div>
  </div>
</section>

Resources Page Code:
Resources Section one:
<!-- DYDD DesignPD Page Body -->
<section class="dypd">
  <div class="dypd-wrap">

 <!-- HERO INTRO -->
<section class="dypd-hero">

  <div class="dypd-logo"
       style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/c88c85b3-b616-4654-87d6-c74df6ca033c/designpd.jpg?format=2500w');">
  </div>

  <h1 class="dypd-title">Move from understanding your design to applying it with clarity</h1>

  <p class="dypd-sub">
    DesignPD helps you understand how you naturally <strong>Plan, Decide, and Do</strong>. Built on the foundation of
    DesignID, it brings your design into everyday life so you can see how your tendencies influence leadership,
    teamwork, decision making, and sustainable contribution.
  </p>

  <!-- Scripture Block -->
  <div class="dypd-verse">
    <p>
      “Commit to the Lord whatever you do, and he will establish your plans.”
    </p>
    <span>Proverbs 16:3</span>
  </div>

  <!-- Soft Requirement Note -->
  <div class="dypd-requirement">
    DesignPD is designed to build on the foundation of DesignID. If you have not yet completed your DesignID assessment,
    that is the best place to begin before exploring your DesignPD report.
  </div>

  <!-- CTA Buttons -->
  <div class="dypd-actions">
    <a class="dypd-btn dypd-btnPrimary" href="https://www.discoverdivine.design/designpd-assessment">
      Get the DesignPD Report <span class="dypd-arrow">→</span>
    </a>
    <a class="dypd-btn" href="https://www.discoverdivine.design/designid-assessment">
      Start with DesignID
    </a>
  </div>

</section>

    <!-- WHAT DESIGNPD IS -->
    <section class="dypd-section">
      <div class="dypd-split dypd-splitTight">
        <div class="dypd-text">
          <div class="dypd-kicker">What Is DesignPD?</div>
          <h2 class="dypd-h2">A practical next step after DesignID</h2>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            DesignID helps you understand the way God’s design is reflected through you. It gives language to identity,
            reflection, and contribution. DesignPD takes the next step by helping you understand how that design tends
            to move in everyday life.
          </p>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            The <strong>PD</strong> in DesignPD can be understood as both <strong>Personal Development</strong> and
            <strong>Professional Development</strong>. The same tendencies that shape how you approach planning,
            decisions, and action at work also shape how you lead, relate, serve, and carry responsibility in the rest of life.
          </p>

          <p class="dypd-p">
            In that sense, DesignPD is where design becomes practical. It helps you see how your inner wiring becomes
            visible in your real patterns, especially when expectations rise, pressure builds, or collaboration becomes complex.
          </p>
        </div>

        <div class="dypd-sideArt">
          <div class="dypd-iconPanel">
            <div class="dypd-icon"
                 style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/b7a300e4-fe78-407a-abb5-290e0ff5c149/designpd-icon.png?format=2500w');">
            </div>
            <div class="dypd-iconCopy">
              <h3>Plan. Decide. Do.</h3>
              <p>
                Three simple movements that reveal how people naturally approach vision, choices, and execution.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

<!-- WHY DESIGNID FIRST -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <div class="dypd-highlight">
    <header class="dypd-head">
      <div class="dypd-kicker">Why DesignID Comes First</div>
      <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">DesignPD is strongest when it grows out of DesignID</h2>
      <p class="dypd-headSub">
        DesignPD is not a replacement for DesignID. It is a companion report that helps you apply what DesignID reveals.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dypd-grid2">
      <article class="dypd-miniCard dypd-miniCard-icon">
        <div class="dypd-miniIcon">
          <img src="https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/ca9324a6-b779-495d-bc73-a6cc667175e1/ID-icon-color+400.jpg?format=2500w" alt="DesignID icon">
        </div>

        <h3 class="dypd-h3">DesignID gives you the foundation</h3>
        <p class="dypd-p">
          DesignID helps you understand your reflections, integrative strengths, and bandwidth patterns. It answers
          the question, <strong>How has God designed me?</strong>
        </p>
      </article>

      <article class="dypd-miniCard dypd-miniCard-icon">
        <div class="dypd-miniIcon">
          <img src="https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/b7a300e4-fe78-407a-abb5-290e0ff5c149/designpd-icon.png?format=2500w" alt="DesignPD icon">
        </div>

        <h3 class="dypd-h3">DesignPD shows how that design moves</h3>
        <p class="dypd-p">
          DesignPD shows how your design tends to show up in action. It answers the question,
          <strong>How do I naturally plan, decide, and act?</strong>
        </p>
      </article>
    </div>

    <p class="dypd-p dypd-centerText">
      Together, they create a far more complete picture. DesignID gives you the language of design. DesignPD shows how that
      design is likely to function in leadership, teamwork, conflict, collaboration, and day to day responsibility.
    </p>
  </div>
</section>

    <!-- STORY ARC -->
    <section class="dypd-section">
      <header class="dypd-head">
        <div class="dypd-kicker">From Insight to Action</div>
        <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Why progression from DesignID to DesignPD is so powerful</h2>
        <p class="dypd-headSub">
          Many people can recognize parts of their design once they see their DesignID results. The next challenge is learning
          how that design actually operates in real life.
        </p>
      </header>

      <div class="dypd-storyGrid">
        <article class="dypd-storyCard">
          <div class="dypd-step">1</div>
          <h3>See your design</h3>
          <p>
            DesignID helps you understand the reflections, blends, and strengths that shape how grace is expressed through your life.
          </p>
        </article>

        <article class="dypd-storyCard">
          <div class="dypd-step">2</div>
          <h3>Name your tendencies</h3>
          <p>

<!-- THE THREE AXES -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <header class="dypd-head">
    <div class="dypd-kicker">The Three Core Movements</div>
    <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Plan, Decide, and Do</h2>
    <p class="dypd-headSub">
      DesignPD centers around three simple but powerful movements. Every person engages in all three, but each person tends
      to approach them a little differently. These patterns shape how you prepare, process, and move.
    </p>
  </header>

  <div class="dypd-axisStack">

    <!-- PLAN -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-plan">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-plan">PLAN</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you approach vision and execution</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-plan">
          <span>Dreamer</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Doer</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Plan axis looks at how you naturally approach preparation, momentum, and forward movement. Some people begin
          with imagination, possibilities, and future vision. Others begin with action, structure, and practical next steps.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Neither side is better. Dreamers help open possibilities. Doers help bring movement and traction. DesignPD helps
          you understand where you tend to begin and how that tendency affects the way you lead, prepare, and contribute.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-plan">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your planning tendency affects how you handle goals, priorities, meetings, change,
          and the pace at which ideas become action.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/3fb2e85d-d272-4f9f-9d0d-d7a21a1c5a2d/diverse-group-of-young-business-people-working-in-2026-03-18-05-03-41-utc+800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

    <!-- DECIDE -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-decide">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-decide">DECIDE</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you process choices and make decisions</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-decide">
          <span>Feel It</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Think It</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Decide axis looks at how you tend to process information when choices need to be made. Some people lead with
          instinct, empathy, and internal awareness. Others lead with analysis, objectivity, and careful evaluation.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Healthy decisions need both discernment and clarity. DesignPD helps reveal where you naturally start, which often
          explains why certain decisions feel obvious to you while others require more effort, more input, or more time.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-decide">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your decision tendency affects how you weigh options, handle tension, respond to people,
          and navigate moments where conviction and complexity meet.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/fc5e805d-692c-4e1a-ad30-d0280f5f760d/stressed-business-colleagues-having-a-meeting-in-a-2026-03-24-23-47-32-utc800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

    <!-- DO -->
    <article class="dypd-axisFeature dypd-axisFeature-do">
      <div class="dypd-axisText">
        <div class="dypd-axisBadge dypd-axisBadge-do">DO</div>
        <h3 class="dypd-axisTitle">How you move work forward</h3>

        <div class="dypd-axisBar dypd-axisBar-do">
          <span>Solo</span>
          <div class="dypd-axisLine"></div>
          <span>Together</span>
        </div>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          The Do axis looks at how you tend to carry responsibility and complete what is in front of you. Some people gain
          momentum through independent ownership. Others gain momentum through shared effort and collaboration.
        </p>

        <p class="dypd-p">
          Both styles bring value. Solo tendencies often create speed and ownership. Together tendencies often create shared
          clarity, stronger buy in, and broader engagement. DesignPD helps make those patterns visible so they can become strengths
          instead of friction points.
        </p>

        <div class="dypd-noteBox dypd-noteBox-do">
          <strong>Why it matters:</strong> Your doing tendency affects communication, delegation, follow through, accountability,
          and the way you contribute inside teams and relationships.
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="dypd-axisMedia">
        <div class="dypd-sideImg dypd-sideCover"
             style="background-image:url('https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/685da500fbad741e29c08c78/96377b09-83ad-43d3-b83a-2cc50a6754ba/surfing-the-web-for-something-to-add-to-his-busine-2026-01-09-11-04-42-utc800.jpg?format=2500w');">
        </div>
      </div>
    </article>

  </div>
</section>

 <!-- PRACTICAL APPLICATIONS -->

      are the environments where your patterns often become most visible and most valuable to understand.
    </p>
  </header>

            DesignPD helps individuals understand why certain ways of working feel natural, why certain responsibilities feel heavier,

            communicate with greater clarity, and grow more intentionally.

<!-- FAQ SECTION -->
<section class="dypd-section">
  <div class="dypd-faqWrap">
    <header class="dypd-head">
      <div class="dypd-kicker">Frequently Asked Questions</div>
      <h2 class="dypd-h2 center">Questions about DesignPD</h2>
      <p class="dypd-headSub">
        A few helpful answers before you begin your DesignPD report.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dypd-faqList">

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Do I need to complete DesignID before DesignPD?</summary>
        <p>
          Yes. DesignPD is designed to build on the foundation of DesignID. DesignID helps you understand your design,
          while DesignPD helps you understand how that design tends to show up in planning, decision making, and action.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>What does DesignPD measure?</summary>
        <p>
          DesignPD explores how you naturally Plan, Decide, and Do. It looks at tendencies such as vision and execution,
          intuition and analysis, and independent or collaborative action.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Is DesignPD for personal development or professional development?</summary>
        <p>
          It can support both. DesignPD helps individuals grow in self-awareness while also helping leaders and teams
          understand how people work, communicate, decide, and contribute together.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>How can teams use DesignPD?</summary>
        <p>
          Teams can use DesignPD to better understand differences in planning, decision making, collaboration, leadership,
          pressure, and sustainability. This can reduce misunderstanding and support healthier alignment.
        </p>
      </details>

      <details class="dypd-faqItem">
        <summary>Is DesignPD a personality test?</summary>
        <p>
          No. DesignPD is not meant to label or limit you. It is a reflection tool that helps you recognize patterns in
          how your design tends to move into everyday action.
        </p>
      </details>

    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<style>

.dydd-blog-filter{
text-align:center;
margin-bottom:30px;
font-size:18px;
}

/* link styling */
.dydd-blog-filter a{
text-decoration:none;
color:#555;
font-weight:500;
padding:0 8px;
}

/* separators */
.dydd-blog-filter span{
color:#bbb;
padding:0 6px;
}

/* acronym letter */
.dydd-blog-filter .acronym{
font-weight:700;
font-size:1.15em;
color:#000;
}

/* hover */
.dydd-blog-filter a:hover{
color:#4A6239;
}

/* active category */
.dydd-blog-filter a.active{
color:#4A6239;
border-bottom:2px solid #4A6239;
padding-bottom:2px;
}

</style>

<script>
const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const category = params.get('category');

if(category){
document.querySelectorAll('.dydd-blog-filter a').forEach(link=>{
if(link.href.includes("category="+category)){
link.classList.add('active');
}
});
}
</script>

Section 2:
<!-- DYDD Live FAQ Accordion -->
<section class="dyfaq">
  <div class="dyfaq-wrap">

    <header class="dyfaq-head">
      <h2 class="dyfaq-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
      <p class="dyfaq-sub">
        A few quick answers to help you understand how DYDD Live works and whether it’s the right fit for your group.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dyfaq-list">

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Who is Discover Your Divine Design Live for?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Discover Your Divine Design Live is designed for individuals, small groups, church teams, ministries, and organizations who want to grow in faith, gain clarity, and better understand how God has uniquely designed them to serve.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">How long is the program and what formats are available?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          DYDD Live is flexible and can be delivered in several formats, including a one-day intensive, a series of Saturday sessions, or a 4-, 6-, or 8-week evening experience. Each format includes live teaching, discussion, and guided application.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">What do participants receive during the experience?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Participants receive live teaching, visual presentation content, guided discussion, and practical tools for reflection and application. Depending on the format, this may also include the book, workbook, assessments, and supporting materials.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Can we host this at our church or organization?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Yes. DYDD Live is designed to be hosted by churches, ministries, and organizations. We work with you to shape the schedule, format, and experience so it fits your people, your setting, and your goals.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">What topics are covered in the DYDD Live sessions?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          The journey covers six core areas: Identity, Expertise, Story, Desire, Spiritual Gifts, and Niche. Together, these themes help participants see how God has been shaping their life and calling.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">What should participants do to prepare?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Preparation depends on the format of your event. In some cases, participants may be invited to complete an assessment or review selected materials in advance, but this is not always required. Any recommended preparation will be communicated clearly before the experience begins.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Is there a minimum or maximum group size?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          DYDD Live can be adapted for a wide range of group sizes, from smaller gatherings to larger church or organizational events. We tailor the structure, discussion flow, and delivery to fit your audience and setting.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Can this be used as part of a discipleship or leadership development program?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Absolutely. Many churches and organizations use DYDD Live as a strong foundation for discipleship, leadership development, team growth, and ministry alignment.
        </div>
      </details>

    </div>

  </div>
</section>

Section 2:
<!-- DYDD Online FAQ -->
<section class="dyfaq">
  <div class="dyfaq-wrap">

    <header class="dyfaq-head">
      <h2 class="dyfaq-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
      <p class="dyfaq-sub">
        Here are a few common questions about the Discover Your Divine Design Online experience.
      </p>
    </header>

    <div class="dyfaq-list">

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">How does DYDD Online work?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Discover Your Divine Design Online is a self-paced course accessible from anywhere. 
          Participants move through video lessons, written reflections, interactive exercises, 
          and downloadable resources designed to guide them through the full DYDD journey.
          <br><br>
          Each module builds on the previous one, helping you explore Identity, Expertise, Story, 
          Desire, Spiritual Gifts, and Niche in a thoughtful and practical way.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Do I have to take the course at a specific time?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          No. DYDD Online is designed to be flexible and self-paced. You can begin when you are ready 
          and move through the material at a pace that works best for you.
          <br><br>
          Some participants move through the content quickly, while others prefer to take more time 
          to reflect, pray, and process each section.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Can I take the course with others?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          Yes. While many people take the course individually, DYDD Online also works well in a 
          group setting such as a small group, ministry team, or church class.
          <br><br>
          Discussion prompts and reflection exercises make it easy for groups to process what they 
          are learning together.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Do I need the book or workbook?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          The online course is designed to work alongside the 
          <strong>Discover Your Divine Design</strong> book and workbook, 
          which provide deeper reflection and guided exercises.
          <br><br>
          It is strongly recommended that each participant have a personal copy 
          of both the book and the workbook while taking the course.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">Are the DesignID™ and Spiritual Gifts assessments required?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          No. The course can be completed without them.
          <br><br>
          However, participants are encouraged to take the 
          <strong>DesignID™ Assessment</strong> and the 
          <strong>Spiritual Gifts Assessment</strong> as they provide helpful insight 
          that complements the learning experience.
        </div>
      </details>

      <details class="dyfaq-item">
        <summary class="dyfaq-question">What will I have when I finish?</summary>
        <div class="dyfaq-answer">
          By the end of the course, participants will have a clearer understanding of how their 
          identity, experiences, passions, and gifts fit together.
          <br><br>
          Many participants also complete a personal 
          <strong>Ministry Declaration</strong>, helping articulate how they sense 
          God calling them to contribute and serve.
        </div>
      </details>

    </div>

  </div>
</section>
